					random_dynasty_member = {

							limit = { NOT = { year = 8120 } }
							add_lover = ROOT
							if = {
								limit = { is_ruler = yes }
								ROOT = { 
									move_character = PREV 
									add_consort = PREV
								}
							}
							if = {
								limit = { 
									is_ruler = no 
									NOT = { year = 8105 }
								}
								liege = {
									ROOT = { 
										move_character = PREV 
									}
								}

			}
